      ,[idOficina]
      ,[idCliente]
      ,[Periodo]
      ,[idConcepto]
      ,[Cantidad]
      ,[ImporteUnit]
      ,[ImporteTotal]
      ,[FAlta]
      ,[UAlta]
      ,[FProceso]
      ,[UProceso]
      ,[IdServicioALiquidar]
  FROM [tributos].[dbo].[RV_SubdiarioOficinas]
  WHERE idCliente = 8037

ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND

M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND

M.FECHA_DEMANDA, E.COD_ESTADO, MA.DENOAM NOM_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION, M.CUIJ_J, 
M.COD_SISTEMA, M.COD_CANCELAC, M.FECHA_CANCEL, M.TIPOJUICIO
FROM M10NAPLEG M
JOIN M10ESTJU E
ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
E.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO 
JOIN M00TABMA MA
ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999 AND
M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '23/10/2025' AND
M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND
M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
(CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
FETCH FIRST 100 ROWS ONLY
---

SELECT DISTINCT M.COD_COMUNA COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA JUZGADONRO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC FECHA_TRAMITE, 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA, E.COD_ESTADO, MA.DENOAM NOM_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION COMENTARIO, M.CUIJ_J, 
M.COD_SISTEMA, M.COD_CANCELAC, M.FECHA_CANCEL, M.TIPOJUICIO
FROM M10NAPLEG M
JOIN M10ESTJU E
ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
E.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO 
JOIN M00TABMA MA
ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999 AND
M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '23/10/2025' AND
M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND
M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
(CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
---
SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT 
        M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA,
        M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA,
        M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO,
        M."AÑO_DEMANDA",
        M.NRO_JUICIO,
        M.FECHA_DEMANDA,
        E.COD_ESTADO,
        MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
        M.CUIJ_J,
        E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M."AÑO_DEMANDA", M.NRO_JUICIO
            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10ESTJU E
      ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA
     AND E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION
     AND E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA
     AND E.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
     AND E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
    JOIN M00TABMA MA
      ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
     AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2020-01-01') AND DATE('2025-10-27')
      AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
      AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = DATE('1900-01-01')
      AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
      AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = DATE('1900-01-01')
) T
WHERE RN = 1;

---
SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT 
        M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA,
        M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA,
        M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO,
        M."AÑO_DEMANDA",
        M.NRO_JUICIO,
        M.FECHA_DEMANDA,
        E.COD_ESTADO,
        MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
        M.CUIJ_J,
        E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M."AÑO_DEMANDA", M.NRO_JUICIO

      ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA
     AND E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION
     AND E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA

    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '27/10/2025'

      ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
     AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '27/10/2025'
      AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
      AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
      AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
      AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
) T
WHERE RN = 1;

    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10ESTJU E
      ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA
     AND E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION
     AND E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA
     AND E.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
     AND E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
    JOIN M00TABMA MA
      ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
     AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '27/10/2025'
      AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
      AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
      AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
      AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
---
SELECT 
        M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA,
        M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA,
        M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO,
        M.AÑO_DEMANDA,
        M.NRO_JUICIO,
        M.FECHA_DEMANDA,
        E.COD_ESTADO,
        MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
        M.CUIJ_J,
        E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO
            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10ESTJU E
      ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA
     AND E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION
     AND E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA

     AND E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO

      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'

SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT 
        M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA,
        M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA,
        M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO,
        M.AÑO_DEMANDA,
        M.NRO_JUICIO,
        M.FECHA_DEMANDA,
        E.COD_ESTADO,
        MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
        M.CUIJ_J,
        E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO
            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10ESTJU E
      ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA
     AND E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION
     AND E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA
     AND E.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
     AND E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
    JOIN M00TABMA MA
      ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
     AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '27/10/2025'
      AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
      AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
      AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
      AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
) T
WHERE RN = 1;

     AND E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO

      ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
     AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '15/09/2018' AND '29/10/2025'
      AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
      AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
      AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
      AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'

        M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA,
        M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA,
        M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO,
        M.AÑO_DEMANDA,
        M.NRO_JUICIO,
        M.FECHA_DEMANDA,
        E.COD_ESTADO,

     AND E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION
     AND E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA
     AND E.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
     AND E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
    JOIN M00TABMA MA
      ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
     AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
      AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '15/09/2018' AND '29/10/2025'
      AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
      AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
      AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
      AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
      AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
---
SELECT 
    M.COD_COMUNA         AS COMUNA,
    M.COD_JURISDICCION   AS INSTANCIA,
    M.COD_INSTANCIA      AS JUZGADONRO,
    M.AÑO_DEMANDA,
    M.NRO_JUICIO,
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA,
    E.COD_ESTADO,
    MA.DENOAM            AS NOM_ESTADO,
    E.DESCRIPCION        AS COMENTARIO,
    M.CUIJ_J,
    E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC   AS FECHA_TRAMITE
FROM M10NAPLEG M
JOIN M10ESTJU E
  ON E.CODCOMUNA     = M.COD_COMUNA
 AND E.JURISDICCION  = M.COD_JURISDICCION
 AND E.INSTANCIA     = M.COD_INSTANCIA
 AND E.ANODEMANDA    = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
 AND E.NROJUICIO     = M.NRO_JUICIO
WHERE E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC = (
    SELECT MAX(E2.FECHATRAMITEJUIC)
    FROM M10ESTJU E2
    WHERE E2.CODCOMUNA     = E.CODCOMUNA
      AND E2.JURISDICCION  = E.JURISDICCION
      AND E2.INSTANCIA     = E.INSTANCIA
      AND E2.ANODEMANDA    = E.ANODEMANDA
      AND E2.NROJUICIO     = E.NROJUICIO
)
AND M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999
AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '2018-09-15' AND '2025-10-29'
AND (M.COD_CANCELAC = '' OR M.COD_CANCELAC IS NULL)
AND M.FECHA_CANCEL = '1900-01-01'
AND M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
AND (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10
AND E.FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
JOIN M00TABMA MA
  ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 
 AND MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO;

---
SELECT * FROM (
SELECT M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, E.COD_ESTADO, MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, M.CUIJ_J, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.CUIJ_J
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
 
FROM M10NAPLEG M 
JOIN M10ESTJU E 
ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND 
E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION AND 
E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
E.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND 
E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO 
JOIN M00TABMA MA 
ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 AND 
MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO 
WHERE 
M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999 AND 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '15/09/2018' AND '29/10/2025' AND 
M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND 
M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND 
M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND 
(CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND 
E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1
---
SELECT * FROM (
SELECT M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, E.COD_ESTADO, MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, M.CUIJ_J, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.CUIJ_J
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
 
FROM M10NAPLEG M 
JOIN M10ESTJU E 
ON E.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND 
E.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION AND 
E.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
E.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND 
E.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO 
JOIN M00TABMA MA 
ON MA.CODPRIN = 452 AND 
MA.SUBCOD = E.COD_ESTADO 
WHERE 
M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999 AND 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '15/09/2018' AND '29/10/2025' AND 
M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND 
M.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND 
M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND 
(CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND 
E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, TIPOJUICIO, CUIJ_J 
FROM M10NAPLEG
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '2025-10-01' AND '2025-11-01' AND
TIPOJUICIO = ''
---

WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '2025-10-01' AND '2025-11-01' AND
TIPOJUICIO = ''
---

TIPOJUICIO = ''

ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
J.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
J.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
J.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
LEFT JOIN M10TABCLA T
ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
T.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND
M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '2025-10-01' AND '2025-11-30' AND
M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
M.TIPOJUICIO = '';

SELECT 
    RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_JURISDICCION)) AS NRO_JUICIO_COMPLETO,
    M.COD_COMUNA, 
    M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, 
    M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, 
    M."AÑO_DEMANDA", 
    M.NRO_JUICIO, 
    M.COD_SISTEMA, 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA, 
    M.MONTO_INICIAL, 
    M.TIPOJUICIO, 
    M.CUIJ_J, 
    J.DESCRIPCION, 
    J.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
FROM M10NAPLEG M
LEFT JOIN M10ESTJU J
    ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION 
   AND J.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA 
   AND J.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND J.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
LEFT JOIN M10TABCLA T
    ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA
   AND T.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1
  AND M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
  AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2025-10-01') AND DATE('2025-11-30')
  AND M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999
  AND (M.TIPOJUICIO = '' OR M.TIPOJUICIO IS NULL)

    RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_JURISDICCION)) AS Nro_Juicio_Instancia, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, 
    M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M."AÑO_DEMANDA", M.NRO_JUICIO, 
    M.COD_SISTEMA, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, M.TIPOJUICIO, M.CUIJ_J, J.DESCRIPCION, J.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
FROM M10NAPLEG M
LEFT JOIN M10ESTJU J
    ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION 
   AND J.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA 
   AND J.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND J.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
LEFT JOIN M10TABCLA T
    ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA
   AND T.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1
  AND M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
  AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2025-10-01') AND DATE('2025-11-30')
  AND M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999
  AND (M.TIPOJUICIO = '' OR M.TIPOJUICIO IS NULL);

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, TIPOJUICIO, CUIJ_J 
FROM M10NAPLEG
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '2025-10-01' AND '2025-11-30' AND
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
TIPOJUICIO = '';

SELECT * FROM M10TABCLA 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND
DESCRIPCION BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NROJUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
ANODEMANDA BETWEEN 2025 AND 2025;

    ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION

    RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_JURISDICCION)) AS Nro_Juicio_Instancia, M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS F_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO,
    M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
    M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M."AÑO_DEMANDA", M.NRO_JUICIO, 
    M.COD_SISTEMA, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, M.TIPOJUICIO, M.CUIJ_J, J.DESCRIPCION, J.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
FROM M10NAPLEG M
LEFT JOIN M10ESTJU J
    ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION 
   AND J.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA 
   AND J.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND J.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
LEFT JOIN M10TABCLA C
    ON C.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND C.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA
   AND C.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND C.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
LEFT JOIN M00TABMA T
    ON T.CODPRIN = 527 
   AND T.SUBCOD = CAST(SUBSTR(TRIM(C.NROACTAS), 1, 3) AS INTEGER)
WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1
  AND M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
  AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2025-10-01') AND DATE('2025-11-30')
  AND M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999
  AND (M.TIPOJUICIO = '' OR M.TIPOJUICIO IS NULL);

    RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_JURISDICCION)) AS Nro_Juicio_Instancia, M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS F_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO,

    ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION

   AND C.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND C.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO

  AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2025-10-01') AND DATE('2025-11-30')

NROJUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
ANODEMANDA BETWEEN 2025 AND 2025;

FROM M10ESTJU
WHERE CODCOMUNA = 1 AND
JURISDICCION BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NROJUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99;

FROM  M10NAPLEG
WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND

SELECT 
    RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(COD_JURISDICCION)) AS Nro_Juicio_Instancia, FECHA_DEMANDA AS F_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO,
    CUIJ_J AS CUIJ
FROM M10NAPLEG 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1
  AND COD_JURISDICCION = 0
  AND BETWEEN 1 AND 9
  AND FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2025-10-01') AND DATE('2025-11-30')
  AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999
  AND TIPOJUICIO = '';



SELECT * FROM M00TABCLA
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
DESCRIPCION 0
COD_JUZGADO BETWEEN 

WHERE COMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, AÑO; JUICIO

SELECT 
    RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_JURISDICCION)) AS Nro_Juicio_Instancia, M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS F_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO,
    M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
    M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M."AÑO_DEMANDA", M.NRO_JUICIO, 
    M.COD_SISTEMA, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, M.TIPOJUICIO, M.CUIJ_J, J.DESCRIPCION, J.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
FROM M10NAPLEG M
LEFT JOIN M10ESTJU J
    ON J.CODCOMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND J.JURISDICCION = M.COD_JURISDICCION 
   AND J.INSTANCIA = M.COD_INSTANCIA 
   AND J.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND J.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
LEFT JOIN M10TABCLA C
    ON C.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA 
   AND C.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA
   AND C.ANODEMANDA = M."AÑO_DEMANDA"
   AND C.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO
WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1
  AND M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
  AND M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN DATE('2025-10-01') AND DATE('2025-11-30')
  AND M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999
  AND (M.TIPOJUICIO = '' OR M.TIPOJUICIO IS NULL);

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, TIPOJUICIO, CUIJ_J 
FROM M10NAPLEG
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '2025-10-01' AND '2025-11-30' AND
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
TIPOJUICIO = '';

WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND

SELECT TABLA2.COD_COMUNA, TABLA2.COD_JUZGADO, TABLA2.DESCRIPCION, TABLA2.ANODEMANDA, TABLA2.NROJUICIO 
FROM (select  M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL>'01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END  AS ESTADO
from (sELECT  M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO,  M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL   FROM  M10TABCLA WHERE  M10TABCLA.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' and  M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL between '01/01/2017' and '26/07/2017'  and    M10TABCLA.CODSISTEMA between 0 and 99 ) as tabla,  M10TABCLA
where  TABLA.COD_COMUNA= M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA  AND  TABLA.COD_JUZGADO= M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO AND  TABLA.DESCRIPCION=  M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION AND  TABLA.ANODEMANDA=  M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA AND  TABLA.NROJUICIO =  M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO) AS TABLA2
GROUP BY TABLA2.COD_COMUNA, TABLA2.COD_JUZGADO, TABLA2.DESCRIPCION, TABLA2.ANODEMANDA, TABLA2.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(TABLA2.ESTADO) >0 AND  SUM(TABLA2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*)
---
SELECT TABLA2.COD_COMUNA, TABLA2.COD_JUZGADO, TABLA2.DESCRIPCION, TABLA2.ANODEMANDA, TABLA2.NROJUICIO 
FROM (SELECT M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL>'01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END  AS ESTADO
FROM (SELECT M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO,  M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL   
FROM M10TABCLA 
WHERE M10TABCLA.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND M10TABCLA.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99 ) as TABLA, M10TABCLA
where  TABLA.COD_COMUNA= M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA AND TABLA.COD_JUZGADO= M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO AND  TABLA.DESCRIPCION=  M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION AND  TABLA.ANODEMANDA=  M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA AND  TABLA.NROJUICIO =  M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO) AS TABLA2
GROUP BY TABLA2.COD_COMUNA, TABLA2.COD_JUZGADO, TABLA2.DESCRIPCION, TABLA2.ANODEMANDA, TABLA2.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(TABLA2.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(TABLA2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*)
---
SELECT B.COD_COMUNA, B.COD_JUZGADO, B.DESCRIPCION, B.ANODEMANDA, B.NROJUICIO 
FROM (SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN M.FECHA_CANCEL >'01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
FROM (SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO, M.FECHA_CANCEL FROM M10TABCLA M
WHERE M10TABCLA.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND M10TABCLA.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99 ) AS A, M10TABCLA
WHERE A.COD_COMUNA= M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA AND A.COD_JUZGADO = M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO AND A.DESCRIPCION = M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION AND A.ANODEMANDA = M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA 
AND A.NROJUICIO = M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO) AS B
GROUP BY B.COD_COMUNA, B.COD_JUZGADO, B.DESCRIPCION, B.ANODEMANDA, B.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(B.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(B.ESTADO) < COUNT(*)
---
SELECT B.COD_COMUNA, B.COD_JUZGADO, B.DESCRIPCION, B.ANODEMANDA, B.NROJUICIO 
FROM (SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN M.FECHA_CANCEL >'01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
FROM (SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO, M.FECHA_CANCEL FROM M10TABCLA AS M
WHERE M10TABCLA.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND M10TABCLA.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99 ) AS A, M10TABCLA
WHERE A.COD_COMUNA= M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA AND A.COD_JUZGADO = M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO AND A.DESCRIPCION = M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION AND A.ANODEMANDA = M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA 
AND A.NROJUICIO = M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO) AS B
GROUP BY B.COD_COMUNA, B.COD_JUZGADO, B.DESCRIPCION, B.ANODEMANDA, B.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(B.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(B.ESTADO) < COUNT(*)

SELECT RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_INSTANCIA)) AS NRO_JUICIO_INSTANCIA, 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.COD_SISTEMA
FROM M10NAPLEG M
JOIN M10TABCLA T
ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
T.DESCRIPCION = M-COD_INSTANCIA AND
T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND

M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
M.TIPOJUICIO = ''

ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND

SELECT RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_INSTANCIA)) AS NRO_JUICIO_INSTANCIA, 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.COD_SISTEMA, T.CODSISTEMA, T.NROACTAS
FROM M10NAPLEG M
JOIN M10TABCLA T
ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
T.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO AND 
T.FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
M.TIPOJUICIO = ''

SELECT RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_INSTANCIA)) AS NRO_JUICIO_INSTANCIA, 
M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, T.CODSISTEMA, T.NROACTAS
FROM M10NAPLEG M
JOIN M10TABCLA T
ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
T.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO AND

SELECT TABLE_SCHEMA, TABLE_NAME 
                                FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES 
                                WHERE TABLE_TYPE = 'BASE TABLE'
                                ORDER BY TABLE_SCHEMA, TABLE_NAME

SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY FECHA_DE_ALTA desc) AS RN,
            NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, COD_COMUNA,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_JURISDICCION AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_JURISDICCION ,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_INSTANCIA AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_INSTANCIA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(AÑO_DEMANDA AS CHAR(10))), '') AÑO_DEMANDA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(NRO_JUICIO, 12, 0))), '') NRO_JUICIO, 
            TIPODOC, NRODOC, CODCALLE AS CALLE, NROPUERTA, 
            COD_POSTAL AS LOCALIDAD, TIPOJUICIO, MONTO_INICIAL, 
            USUARIO_ALTA, FECHA_DE_ALTA, HORA_DEL_ALTA, FECHA_DECRETO, COD_SISTEMA 
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE LENGTH(LTRIM(RTRIM(COD_CANCELAC))) = 0 
        AND FECHA_CANCEL = ? 
        AND NRO_CONVENIO = ? 
        AND TIPOJUICIO = ? 
        AND FECHA_DE_ALTA BETWEEN CURRENT DATE - 2 YEARS AND CURRENT DATE
        
) AS T 
WHERE RN BETWEEN ? AND ?
---
SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY FECHA_DE_ALTA desc) AS RN,
            NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, COD_COMUNA,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_JURISDICCION AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_JURISDICCION ,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_INSTANCIA AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_INSTANCIA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(AÑO_DEMANDA AS CHAR(10))), '') AÑO_DEMANDA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(NRO_JUICIO, 12, 0))), '') NRO_JUICIO, 
            TIPODOC, NRODOC, CODCALLE AS CALLE, NROPUERTA, 
            COD_POSTAL AS LOCALIDAD, TIPOJUICIO, MONTO_INICIAL, 
            USUARIO_ALTA, FECHA_DE_ALTA, HORA_DEL_ALTA, FECHA_DECRETO, COD_SISTEMA 
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE LENGTH(LTRIM(RTRIM(COD_CANCELAC))) = 0 
        AND FECHA_CANCEL = '' 
        AND NRO_CONVENIO = ? 
        AND TIPOJUICIO = ? 
        AND FECHA_DE_ALTA BETWEEN CURRENT DATE - 2 YEARS AND CURRENT DATE
        
) AS T 
WHERE RN BETWEEN ? AND ?

SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY FECHA_DE_ALTA desc) AS RN,
            NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, COD_COMUNA,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_JURISDICCION AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_JURISDICCION ,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_INSTANCIA AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_INSTANCIA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(AÑO_DEMANDA AS CHAR(10))), '') AÑO_DEMANDA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(NRO_JUICIO, 12, 0))), '') NRO_JUICIO, 
            TIPODOC, NRODOC, CODCALLE AS CALLE, NROPUERTA, 
            COD_POSTAL AS LOCALIDAD, TIPOJUICIO, MONTO_INICIAL, 
            USUARIO_ALTA, FECHA_DE_ALTA, HORA_DEL_ALTA, FECHA_DECRETO, COD_SISTEMA 
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE LENGTH(LTRIM(RTRIM(COD_CANCELAC))) = 0 
        AND FECHA_CANCEL = ? 
        AND NRO_CONVENIO = ? 
        AND TIPOJUICIO = ? 
        AND FECHA_DE_ALTA BETWEEN CURRENT DATE - 2 YEARS AND CURRENT DATE
        
) AS T 
WHERE RN BETWEEN ? AND ?
---
SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY FECHA_DE_ALTA desc) AS RN,
            NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, COD_COMUNA,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_JURISDICCION AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_JURISDICCION ,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_INSTANCIA AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_INSTANCIA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(AÑO_DEMANDA AS CHAR(10))), '') AÑO_DEMANDA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(NRO_JUICIO, 12, 0))), '') NRO_JUICIO, 
            TIPODOC, NRODOC, CODCALLE AS CALLE, NROPUERTA, 
            COD_POSTAL AS LOCALIDAD, TIPOJUICIO, MONTO_INICIAL, 
            USUARIO_ALTA, FECHA_DE_ALTA, HORA_DEL_ALTA, FECHA_DECRETO, COD_SISTEMA 
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE LENGTH(LTRIM(RTRIM(COD_CANCELAC))) = 0 
        AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01-01-1900' 
        AND NRO_CONVENIO = 0 
        AND TIPOJUICIO = '' 
        AND FECHA_DE_ALTA BETWEEN CURRENT DATE - 2 YEARS AND CURRENT DATE
        
) AS T 
WHERE RN BETWEEN 1 AND 20

FROM (
    SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY FECHA_DE_ALTA desc) AS RN,
            NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, COD_COMUNA,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_JURISDICCION AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_JURISDICCION ,
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(COD_INSTANCIA AS CHAR(10))), '') COD_INSTANCIA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CAST(AÑO_DEMANDA AS CHAR(10))), '') AÑO_DEMANDA, 
            COALESCE(RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(NRO_JUICIO, 12, 0))), '') NRO_JUICIO, 
            TIPODOC, NRODOC, CODCALLE AS CALLE, NROPUERTA, 
            COD_POSTAL AS LOCALIDAD, TIPOJUICIO, MONTO_INICIAL, 
            USUARIO_ALTA, FECHA_DE_ALTA, HORA_DEL_ALTA, FECHA_DECRETO, COD_SISTEMA 
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE LENGTH(LTRIM(RTRIM(COD_CANCELAC))) = 0 
        AND NRO_CONVENIO = 0 
        AND TIPOJUICIO = '' 
        AND FECHA_DE_ALTA BETWEEN CURRENT DATE - 2 YEARS AND CURRENT DATE
        
) AS T 
WHERE RN BETWEEN 1 AND 20

            AÑO_DEMANDA, 
            NRO_JUICIO, 
            TIPODOC, NRODOC, CODCALLE AS CALLE, NROPUERTA, 
            COD_POSTAL AS LOCALIDAD, TIPOJUICIO, MONTO_INICIAL, 
            USUARIO_ALTA, FECHA_DE_ALTA, HORA_DEL_ALTA, FECHA_DECRETO, COD_SISTEMA 
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE LENGTH(LTRIM(RTRIM(COD_CANCELAC))) = 0

        AND TIPOJUICIO = ''

FECBAJA = ?

SELECT * FROM APREMIOS.M10JUIBAJAS
WHERE Comuna = 1 AND
jurisdiccion >= 0 AND
jurisdiccion <= 9 AND

instancia <= 9999 AND
añodemanda >= 0 AND

SELECT * FROM (
                                    SELECT M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO,
                                        M.FECHA_DEMANDA, E.COD_ESTADO, MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, M.CUIJ_J, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.CUIJ_J
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10NAPLEG M
                                        WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND
                                        M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND
                                        M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
                                        M.FECHA_CANCEL = ? AND
                                        M.TIPOJUICIO = ? AND
                                        (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= ? AND
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;
---
SELECT * FROM (
                                    SELECT E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10ESTJU E
                                        WHERE (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= ? AND
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;
---

                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10ESTJU E
                                        WHERE (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;

                                    SELECT E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10ESTJU E
                                        WHERE (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;

SELECT * FROM (
                                    SELECT E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10ESTJU E
                                        WHERE (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
E.CODESTADO > 0
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;

SELECT * FROM (
                                    SELECT E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10ESTJU E
                                        WHERE (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
and NROJUICIO = 21242098592
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;

SELECT * FROM (
                                    SELECT E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
                                        ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
                                            PARTITION BY E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
                                            ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                                        ) AS RN
                                        FROM M10ESTJU E
                                        WHERE (CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10 AND
                                        E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900') T WHERE RN = 1;

T WHERE RN = 1;

GROUP BY E.COD_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO
HAVING MAX ((CURRENT DATE - E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) >= 10)
ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC

SELECT M.COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADONRO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO,
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA, E.COD_ESTADO, MA.DENOAM AS NOM_ESTADO, E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, M.CUIJ_J, E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC AS FECHA_TRAMITE,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER(
        PARTITION BY M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.CUIJ_J
        ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
    ) AS RN
    FROM {M10NAPLEGModel.MODELTABNAME} M
    WHERE M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 21242098592 AND 21242098592 AND
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '12/02/2025' AND
    M.COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
    M.FECHA_CANCEL = '1900/01/01' AND
    M.TIPOJUICIO = ''

        ORDER BY E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC

SELECT 
    COD_ESTADO,
    DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
    MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) AS FECHA_TRAMITE
FROM M10ESTJU E
WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
    CODCOMUNA = ? AND
    JURISDICCION = ? AND
    INSTANCIA = ? AND
    ANODEMANDA = ? AND
    NROJUICIO = ?
GROUP BY 
    COD_ESTADO,
    DESCRIPCION
HAVING 
    (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC))) >= ?
ORDER BY 
    MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) DESC;
---
SELECT COD_ESTADO, DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO, MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) AS FECHA_TRAMITE
                            FROM M10ESTJU E
                            WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01' AND 
                                CODCOMUNA = 1 AND
                                JURISDICCION = 1 AND
                                INSTANCIA = 1 AND
                                ANODEMANDA = 2025 AND
                                NROJUICIO = 21242098592
                            GROUP BY 
                                COD_ESTADO,
                                DESCRIPCION
                            HAVING 
                                (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC))) >= 10
                            ORDER BY 
                                MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) DESC
---
SELECT 
    E.COD_ESTADO,
    E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
    MAX(E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) AS FECHA_TRAMITE
FROM M10ESTJU E
WHERE E.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
GROUP BY 
    E.COD_ESTADO,
    E.DESCRIPCION
HAVING 
    (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(MAX(E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC))) >= 10
ORDER BY 
    MAX(E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC) DESC;

    MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) AS FECHA_TRAMITE

WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
GROUP BY 
    COD_ESTADO,
    DESCRIPCION
HAVING 
    (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC))) >= ?
ORDER BY 
    MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) DESC;

SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, 
    COD_ESTADO,
    DESCRIPCION,
    MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC) AS FECHA_TRAMITE
FROM DB2ADMIN.M10ESTJU
WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
NROJUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND
FECHATRAMITEJUIC > ?
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, 
    COD_ESTADO,
    DESCRIPCION
HAVING 
    (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC))) >= ?

SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT
        CODCOMUNA,
        JURISDICCION,
        INSTANCIA,
        ANODEMANDA,
        NROJUICIO,
        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
           PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
           ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM DB2ADMIN.M10ESTJU
    WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
      AND NROJUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ?
      AND FECHATRAMITEJUIC > ?
) X
WHERE RN = 1
  AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= ?
ORDER BY
    CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO;

---
SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT
        CODCOMUNA,
        JURISDICCION,
        INSTANCIA,
        ANODEMANDA,
        NROJUICIO,
        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC,

           PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO

        CODCOMUNA,
        JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA,
        INSTANCIA,
        ANODEMANDA,
        NROJUICIO,
        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
           PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
           ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM M10ESTJU
    WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
      AND NROJUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ?
      AND FECHATRAMITEJUIC >= ?
) X
WHERE RN = 1
  AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= ?
ORDER BY
    CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO;

---
SELECT  E.COD_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
        E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC
FROM    M10ESTJU E
WHERE   E.FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
  AND   E.NROJUICIO  = 10024254
  AND   E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC = (
            SELECT MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)
            FROM   M10ESTJU X
            WHERE  X.FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
              AND  X.NROJUICIO  = E.NROJUICIO
        )
  AND   (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
        E.COD_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION
---
SELECT  COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION AS COMENTARIO,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC
FROM    M10ESTJU 
WHERE   FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
  AND   NROJUICIO  = 10024254
  AND   FECHATRAMITEJUIC = (
            SELECT MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)
            FROM   M10ESTJU X
            WHERE  X.FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
              AND  X.NROJUICIO  = NROJUICIO
        )
  AND   (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION

        E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC

  AND   E.NROJUICIO  = 100
  AND   E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC = (
            SELECT MAX(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)
            FROM   M10ESTJU X
            WHERE  X.FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
              AND  X.NROJUICIO  = E.NROJUICIO
        )
  AND   (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(E.FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
        E.COD_ESTADO,
        E.DESCRIPCION;

---
SELECT *
FROM (
    SELECT
        CODCOMUNA,
        JURISDICCION,
        INSTANCIA,
        ANODEMANDA,
        NROJUICIO,
        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
           PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
           ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM DB2ADMIN.M10ESTJU
    WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
      AND NROJUICIO BETWEEN 0 AND 99999999
      AND FECHATRAMITEJUIC >= '2020-01-01'
) X
WHERE RN = 1
  AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
    CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO;

        JURISDICCION,
        INSTANCIA,
        ANODEMANDA,
        NROJUICIO,
        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
           PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
           ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM DB2ADMIN.M10ESTJU
    WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
      AND NROJUICIO BETWEEN IN (10024254, 100543, 100, 2199999)
      AND FECHATRAMITEJUIC >= '2020-01-01'
) X

  AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
    CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO;

        ANODEMANDA,

        COD_ESTADO,
        DESCRIPCION,
        FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
           PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
           ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
        ) AS RN
    FROM DB2ADMIN.M10ESTJU
    WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
      AND NROJUICIO IN (10024254, 100543, 100, 2199999)
      AND FECHATRAMITEJUIC >= '2020-01-01'
) X
WHERE RN = 1
  AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
    CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO;

        ) AS RN

    WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '1900-01-01'
      AND NROJUICIO = 10024254 AND ANODEMANDA = 2021
) X
WHERE RN = 1
  AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
ORDER BY
    CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO;

SELECT TABLA2.COD_COMUNA, TABLA2.COD_JUZGADO, TABLA2.DESCRIPCION, TABLA2.ANODEMANDA, TABLA2.NROJUICIO 
FROM (select  M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL>'01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END  AS ESTADO
from (sELECT  M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO,  M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL   FROM  M10TABCLA WHERE  M10TABCLA.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' and  M10TABCLA.FECHA_CANCEL between '01/01/2017' and '26/07/2017'  and    M10TABCLA.CODSISTEMA between 0 and 99 ) as tabla,  M10TABCLA
where  TABLA.COD_COMUNA= M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA  AND  TABLA.COD_JUZGADO= M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO AND  TABLA.DESCRIPCION=  M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION AND  TABLA.ANODEMANDA=  M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA AND  TABLA.NROJUICIO =  M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO) AS TABLA2
GROUP BY TABLA2.COD_COMUNA, TABLA2.COD_JUZGADO, TABLA2.DESCRIPCION, TABLA2.ANODEMANDA, TABLA2.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(TABLA2.ESTADO) >0 AND  SUM(TABLA2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*)
---
SELECT T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO 
FROM (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
FROM (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
   FROM M10TABCLA MC 
   WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
   MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
   MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99) AS T,  M10TABCLA MT
WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
      T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
      T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
      T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
      T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO) AS T2
GROUP BY T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(T2.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(T2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*)
---
SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
             FROM M10TABCLA MC 
             WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
             MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
             MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
---
SELECT T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO 
FROM (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
FROM (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
             FROM M10TABCLA MC 
             WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
             MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
             MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99) AS T,  M10TABCLA MT
WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
      T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
      T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
      T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
      T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO) AS T2
GROUP BY T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(T2.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(T2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*);


SELECT DISTINCT 
    A.COD_COMUNA, 
    A.COD_JUZGADO, 
    A.DESCRIPCION, 
    A.ANODEMANDA, 
    A.NROJUICIO
FROM M10TABCLA A
WHERE 
    A.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
AND A.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017'
AND A.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM M10TABCLA B
    WHERE 
        B.COD_COMUNA   = A.COD_COMUNA
    AND B.COD_JUZGADO = A.COD_JUZGADO
    AND B.DESCRIPCION = A.DESCRIPCION
    AND B.ANODEMANDA  = A.ANODEMANDA
    AND B.NROJUICIO   = A.NROJUICIO
    AND B.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
);


SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
             FROM M10TABCLA MC 
             WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
             MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
             MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
---
SELECT T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO 
FROM (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
FROM (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
             FROM M10TABCLA MC 
             WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
             MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
             MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99) AS T,  M10TABCLA MT
WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
      T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
      T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
      T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
      T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO) AS T2
GROUP BY T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(T2.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(T2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*);

             FROM M10TABCLA MC 
             WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
             MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/10/2025' AND '09/12/2025' AND

      T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
      T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND

HAVING SUM(T2.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(T2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*);

WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
COD_JURISDICCION = 1 AND

NRO_JUICIO = 21242108989

SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
  CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
  FROM 
   (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
    FROM M10TABCLA MC 
    WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
    MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
    MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
   ) AS T,  
   M10TABCLA MT
  WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
  T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
  T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
  T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
  T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO
---
SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
  CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
  FROM 
   (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
    FROM M10TABCLA MC 
    WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
    MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
    MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
   ) AS T,  
   M10TABCLA MT
  WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
  T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
  T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
  T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
  T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO
GROUP BY MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(ESTADO) < COUNT(*);

---
SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
  CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
  FROM 
   (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
    FROM M10TABCLA MC 
    WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
    MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
    MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
   ) AS T,  
   M10TABCLA MT
  WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
  T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
  T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
  T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
  T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO
GROUP BY MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0 AND SUM(CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) < COUNT(*);

---
SELECT DISTINCT 
    A.COD_COMUNA, 
    A.COD_JUZGADO, 
    A.DESCRIPCION, 
    A.ANODEMANDA, 
    A.NROJUICIO
FROM M10TABCLA A
WHERE 
    A.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
AND A.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017'
AND A.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99

-- 1) Existe al menos un registro CANCELADO
AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM M10TABCLA C
    WHERE 
        C.COD_COMUNA   = A.COD_COMUNA
    AND C.COD_JUZGADO = A.COD_JUZGADO
    AND C.DESCRIPCION = A.DESCRIPCION
    AND C.ANODEMANDA  = A.ANODEMANDA
    AND C.NROJUICIO   = A.NROJUICIO
    AND C.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900'
)

-- 2) Existe al menos un registro NO CANCELADO
AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM M10TABCLA N
    WHERE 
        N.COD_COMUNA   = A.COD_COMUNA
    AND N.COD_JUZGADO = A.COD_JUZGADO
    AND N.DESCRIPCION = A.DESCRIPCION
    AND N.ANODEMANDA  = A.ANODEMANDA
    AND N.NROJUICIO   = A.NROJUICIO
    AND N.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
);

SELECT T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO FROM 

( 
SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO FROM 
(

SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
FROM M10TABCLA MC 
WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99) AS T, M10TABCLA MT WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO) AS T2 GROUP BY T2.COD_COMUNA, T2.COD_JUZGADO, T2.DESCRIPCION, T2.ANODEMANDA, T2.NROJUICIO HAVING SUM(T2.ESTADO) > 0 AND SUM(T2.ESTADO) < COUNT(*);


SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO, 
  CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS ESTADO
  FROM 
   (SELECT MC.COD_COMUNA, MC.COD_JUZGADO, MC.DESCRIPCION, MC.ANODEMANDA, MC.NROJUICIO, MC.FECHA_CANCEL 
    FROM M10TABCLA MC 
    WHERE MC.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
    MC.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2017' AND '26/07/2017' AND 
    MC.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
   ) AS T,  
   M10TABCLA MT
  WHERE T.COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
  T.COD_JUZGADO = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
  T.DESCRIPCION = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
  T.ANODEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
  T.NROJUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO
GROUP BY MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO
HAVING SUM(CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) > 0 AND SUM(CASE WHEN MT.FECHA_CANCEL > '01/01/1900' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) < COUNT(*);

SELECT DISTINCT A.COD_COMUNA, A.COD_JUZGADO, A.DESCRIPCION, A.ANODEMANDA, A.NROJUICIO
FROM M10TABCLA A
WHERE 
    A.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
AND A.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/10/2025' AND '09/12/2025' 
AND A.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM M10TABCLA B
    WHERE 
        B.COD_COMUNA   = A.COD_COMUNA
    AND B.COD_JUZGADO = A.COD_JUZGADO
    AND B.DESCRIPCION = A.DESCRIPCION
    AND B.ANODEMANDA  = A.ANODEMANDA
    AND B.NROJUICIO   = A.NROJUICIO
    AND B.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
);

WHERE 
    A.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
AND A.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '10/12/2025' 
AND A.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99
AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 
    FROM M10TABCLA B
    WHERE 
        B.COD_COMUNA   = A.COD_COMUNA
    AND B.COD_JUZGADO = A.COD_JUZGADO
    AND B.DESCRIPCION = A.DESCRIPCION
    AND B.ANODEMANDA  = A.ANODEMANDA
    AND B.NROJUICIO   = A.NROJUICIO
    AND B.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
);
---

FROM M10TABCLA A
WHERE 
    A.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
AND A.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '10/12/2025'

SELECT DISTINCT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, 
                                    M.COD_SISTEMA, M.NOMBRE, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, M.COD_CANCELAC, M.FECHA_CANCEL, M.TIPOJUICIO, M.CUIJ_J
                                    FROM M10TABCLA C
                                    JOIN M10NAPLEG M
                                    ON M.COD_COMUNA = C.COD_COMUNA AND
                                       M.COD_JURISDICCION = C.COD_JUZGADO AND
                                       M.COD_INSTANCIA = C.DESCRIPCION AND
                                       M.AÑO_DEMANDA = C.ANODEMANDA AND
                                       M.NRO_JUICIO = C.NROJUICIO
                                    WHERE 
                                        C.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
                                        C.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
                                        M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
                                        C.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '110/12/2025' AND 
                                        C.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 1 AND 99 AND 
                                        EXISTS (
                                                SELECT 1 
                                                FROM M10TABCLA B
                                                WHERE B.COD_COMUNA = C.COD_COMUNA AND 
                                                      B.COD_JUZGADO = C.COD_JUZGADO AND 
                                                      B.DESCRIPCION = C.DESCRIPCION AND 
                                                      B.ANODEMANDA = C.ANODEMANDA AND 
                                                      B.NROJUICIO = C.NROJUICIO AND 
                                                      B.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
                                                )
---
SELECT DISTINCT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, 
                                    M.COD_SISTEMA, M.NOMBRE, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, M.COD_CANCELAC, M.FECHA_CANCEL, M.TIPOJUICIO, M.CUIJ_J
                                    FROM M10TABCLA C
                                    JOIN M10NAPLEG M
                                    ON M.COD_COMUNA = C.COD_COMUNA AND
                                       M.COD_JURISDICCION = C.COD_JUZGADO AND
                                       M.COD_INSTANCIA = C.DESCRIPCION AND
                                       M.AÑO_DEMANDA = C.ANODEMANDA AND
                                       M.NRO_JUICIO = C.NROJUICIO
                                    WHERE 
                                        C.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
                                        C.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND 
                                        M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
                                        C.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '10/12/2025' AND 
                                        C.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 1 AND 99 AND 
                                        EXISTS (
                                                SELECT 1 
                                                FROM M10TABCLA B
                                                WHERE B.COD_COMUNA = C.COD_COMUNA AND 
                                                      B.COD_JUZGADO = C.COD_JUZGADO AND 
                                                      B.DESCRIPCION = C.DESCRIPCION AND 
                                                      B.ANODEMANDA = C.ANODEMANDA AND 
                                                      B.NROJUICIO = C.NROJUICIO AND 
                                                      B.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
                                                )
---
SELECT DISTINCT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION, M.COD_INSTANCIA, M.AÑO_DEMANDA, M.NRO_JUICIO, 
M.COD_SISTEMA, M.NOMBRE, M.FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL, M.COD_CANCELAC, M.FECHA_CANCEL, M.TIPOJUICIO, M.CUIJ_J
FROM M10TABCLA C
JOIN M10NAPLEG M
ON M.COD_COMUNA = C.COD_COMUNA AND
   M.COD_JURISDICCION = C.COD_JUZGADO AND
   M.COD_INSTANCIA = C.DESCRIPCION AND
   M.AÑO_DEMANDA = C.ANODEMANDA AND
   M.NRO_JUICIO = C.NROJUICIO
WHERE 
    C.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
    C.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900' AND
    M.TIPOJUICIO = '' AND 
    C.FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '10/12/2025' AND 
    C.CODSISTEMA BETWEEN 0 AND 99 AND 
    EXISTS (
          SELECT 1 
          FROM M10TABCLA B
          WHERE B.COD_COMUNA = C.COD_COMUNA AND 
                B.COD_JUZGADO = C.COD_JUZGADO AND 
                B.DESCRIPCION = C.DESCRIPCION AND 
                B.ANODEMANDA = C.ANODEMANDA AND 
                B.NROJUICIO = C.NROJUICIO AND 
                B.FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900'
          );

   M.COD_JURISDICCION = C.COD_JUZGADO AND
   M.COD_INSTANCIA = C.DESCRIPCION AND

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 
 COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J
FROM M10NAPLEG 
WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/12/2025' AND 
 COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
        FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/12/2025' AND 
 (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO)  
  IN (
   SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JUZGADO, DESCRIPCION, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                        FROM M10TABCLA
                        WHERE COD_COMUNA = COD_COMUNA AND 
                         COD_JURISDICCION = COD_JUZGADO AND 
                                COD_INSTANCIA = DESCRIPCION AND 
                                AÑO_DEMANDA = ANODEMANDA AND 
                                NRO_JUICIO = NROJUICIO AND 
                                CODSISTEMA = 0
  ) 
ORDER BY FECHA_CANCEL, COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 
 COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J
FROM M10NAPLEG 
WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/12/2025' AND 
 COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
        FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/12/2025' AND 
 (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO)  
  IN (
   SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JUZGADO, DESCRIPCION, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                        FROM M10TABCLA
                        WHERE COD_COMUNA = COD_COMUNA AND 
                         COD_JURISDICCION = COD_JUZGADO AND 
                                COD_INSTANCIA = DESCRIPCION AND 
                                AÑO_DEMANDA = ANODEMANDA AND 
                                NRO_JUICIO = NROJUICIO AND 
                                CODSISTEMA = 1
  ) 
ORDER BY FECHA_CANCEL, COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 
                                COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J
                                FROM M10NAPLEG 
                                WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/12/2025' AND 
                                COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
                                FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/12/2025' AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) 
                                IN (
                                    SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JUZGADO, DESCRIPCION, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    FROM M10TABCLA
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = COD_COMUNA AND 
                                        COD_JURISDICCION = COD_JUZGADO AND 
                                        COD_INSTANCIA = DESCRIPCION AND 
                                        AÑO_DEMANDA = ANODEMANDA AND 
                                        NRO_JUICIO = NROJUICIO AND 
                                        CODSISTEMA = 1) ORDER BY FECHA_CANCEL, COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION

SELECT CODSISTEMA AS CODSISTEMA_CLAVE, NROACTAS AS CLAVESISTEMA, NROJUIINTERNO, MONTOADEUDADO, NRO_CONVENIO, COD_BAJA 
                                                FROM M10TABCLA 
                                                WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND
                                                      COD_JUZGADO = 1 AND
                                                      DESCRIPCION = 5 AND
                                                      ANODEMANDA = 2025 AND

FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (1,2,3,4) AND 
NROJUICIO > 0 AND 
COD_ESTADO > 0 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
HAVING COUNT (*) > 0
---

COD_ESTADO > 0

HAVING COUNT (*) > 0

SELECT SUM(CCTE_IMPOR_DESCON)
FROM M12CCTEMBA
WHERE CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO >= ?
AND CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO <= ?
AND CCTE_LEGAJO >= ?
AND CCTE_LEGAJO <= ?
AND CCTE_NRO_BOL_DEP = 0
AND CCTE_PER_DTO = ? 
AND CCTE_NRORECIPERI BETWEEN '01/12/2025' AND '31/12/2025'
AND ASCII(CCTE_IGNORAR_CONTAB) = 0    
AND CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO
IN (SELECT M.EMB_NRO_EMBARGO FROM M12EMBARGO M
    WHERE M.EMB_NRO_EMBARGO = CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO
    AND M.EMB_DEST_DEPOSITO = '230000'
    AND M.EMB_BCO_CTA_JUDIC = 5
    AND M.EMB_CTA_JUDICIAL > 0)
---
SELECT SUM(CCTE_IMPOR_DESCON)
FROM M12CCTEMBA
WHERE CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO >= 0
AND CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO <= 99999999
AND CCTE_LEGAJO >= 0
AND CCTE_LEGAJO <= 99999
AND CCTE_NRO_BOL_DEP = 0
AND CCTE_PER_DTO BETWEEN '01/12/2025' AND '31/12/2025' 
AND CCTE_NRORECIPERI = 1
AND ASCII(CCTE_IGNORAR_CONTAB) = 0    
AND CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO
IN (SELECT M.EMB_NRO_EMBARGO FROM M12EMBARGO M
    WHERE M.EMB_NRO_EMBARGO = CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO
    AND M.EMB_DEST_DEPOSITO = '230000'
    AND M.EMB_BCO_CTA_JUDIC = 5
    AND M.EMB_CTA_JUDICIAL > 0)

AND CCTE_LEGAJO <= 99999
AND CCTE_NRO_BOL_DEP = 0
AND CCTE_PER_DTO BETWEEN '01/12/2025' AND '31/12/2025' 
AND CCTE_NRORECIPERI = 1
AND ASCII(CCTE_IGNORAR_CONTAB) = 0    
AND CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO
IN (SELECT M.EMB_NRO_EMBARGO FROM M12EMBARGO M
    WHERE M.EMB_NRO_EMBARGO = CCTE_NRO_EMBARGO
    AND M.EMB_DEST_DEPOSITO = '230000'
    AND M.EMB_BCO_CTA_JUDIC = 5
    AND M.EMB_CTA_JUDICIAL > 0)

FROM M12CCTEMBA

SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE COD_ESTADO IN () AND 
                                            NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 0
---
SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE 
                                            NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 0
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA,  MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900', NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, '', FECHA_CANCEL, 0 
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                                    FROM M10ESTJU 
                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > ? AND COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                     
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 0) AS T 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = ?
AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ?
AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? 
AND FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN ? AND ? 
AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ?
AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA
AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = ? AND TIPOJUICIO = 'C'
                                
---

FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO

                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 0) AS T 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = ?
AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ?
AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? 
AND FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN ? AND ? 
AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ?

                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0

SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                                    FROM M10ESTJU 
                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 2
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA,  MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, '' AS VACIO, FECHA_CANCEL, 0 AS MONTO
                                FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                                    FROM M10ESTJU 
                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0 
                                     
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 2) AS T 
                                WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1
                                AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
                                AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 
                                AND FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2004' AND '09/01/2026'
                                AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 0 AND 999999999999.99
                                
                                 AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, 
                MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA
                AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = 0
                                
                                 AND TIPOJUICIO = 'C'
                                )

                                FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                                    FROM M10ESTJU 
                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0 
                                     
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 2) AS T 
                                WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1
                                AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
                                AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 
                                AND FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2004' AND '09/01/2026'
                                AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 0 AND 999999999999
                                
                                 AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, 
                MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA
                AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = 0
                                
                                 AND TIPOJUICIO = 'C'
                                )

                                    FROM M10ESTJU 
                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0

                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE

                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 10

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA,  MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, '' AS VACIO, FECHA_CANCEL, 0 AS MONTO
                                FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                                    FROM M10ESTJU 
                                    WHERE NROJUICIO > 0 AND COD_ESTADO > 0 
                                     
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                    HAVING COUNT(*) = 10) AS T 
                                WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1
                                AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9
                                AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 
                                AND FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2004' AND '09/01/2026'
                                AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 0 AND 999999999999
                                
                                 AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO,

                AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = 0

                                AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9

                                        COD_ESTADO > 0  
                                        GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                                        GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 0) AS T  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                     AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, 
                    MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND

                                        COD_ESTADO > 0

                                        GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 0) AS T  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, 
MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, CHR(0) AS VACIO, FECHA_CANCEL, 0 AS MONTO 
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 0 AND 999999999999.99 
AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
---

SELECT 
  COLNAME AS "Columna",
  TYPENAME AS "Tipo de dato",
  LENGTH,
  SCALE,
  NULLS AS "Permite Nulos"
FROM 
  SYSCAT.COLUMNS
WHERE 
  TABNAME = 'M10NAPLEG'
ORDER BY 
  COLNO;
---

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/10/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                     AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---
SELECT c.name AS Nombre, ty.name AS Tipo, c.max_length AS Longitud, c.scale AS Escala, CASE WHEN c.is_nullable = 1 THEN 'SÍ' ELSE 'NO' END AS AceptaNulos FROM sys.columns c JOIN sys.types ty ON c.user_type_id = ty.user_type_id JOIN sys.tables t ON c.object_id = t.object_id WHERE t.name = 'N19CUEENVAPREMIOS' ORDER BY c.column_id;
---

SELECT 
    c.name AS Nombre, 
    ty.name AS Tipo, 
    c.max_length AS Longitud, 
    c.scale AS Escala, 
    CASE WHEN c.is_nullable = 1 THEN 'SÍ' ELSE 'NO' END AS AceptaNulos 
FROM sys.columns c 
INNER JOIN sys.types ty 
    ON c.user_type_id = ty.user_type_id 
-- Se eliminan duplicados al asegurar que el tipo de usuario coincida exactamente
INNER JOIN sys.tables t 
    ON c.object_id = t.object_id 
WHERE t.name = 'N19CUEENVAPREMIOS' 
ORDER BY c.column_id;
---

    c.name AS Nombre, 
    ty.name AS Tipo, 
    c.max_length AS Longitud,

WHERE t.name = 'N19CUEENVAPREMIOS'

SELECT c.name AS Nombre, ty.name AS Tipo, c.max_length AS Longitud, c.scale AS Escala, CASE WHEN c.is_nullable = 1 THEN 'SÍ' ELSE 'NO' END AS AceptaNulos 
FROM sys.columns c 
LEFT JOIN sys.types ty 
ON c.user_type_id = ty.user_type_id 
LEFT JOIN sys.tables t 
ON c.object_id = t.object_id 
WHERE t.name = 'APREMIOS.N19CUEENVAPREMIOS' 
ORDER BY c.column_id;
---
SELECT c.name AS Nombre, ty.name AS Tipo, c.max_length AS Longitud, c.scale AS Escala, CASE WHEN c.is_nullable = 1 THEN 'SÍ' ELSE 'NO' END AS AceptaNulos, SCHEMA_NAME(t.schema_id) 
FROM sys.columns c 
LEFT JOIN sys.types ty 
ON c.user_type_id = ty.user_type_id 
LEFT JOIN sys.tables t 
ON c.object_id = t.object_id 
WHERE t.name = 'N19CUEENVAPREMIOS' and SCHEMA_NAME(t.schema_id) = 'APREMIOS'
ORDER BY c.column_id;
---
SELECT c.name AS Nombre, ty.name AS Tipo, c.max_length AS Longitud, c.scale AS Escala, CASE WHEN c.is_nullable = 1 THEN 'SÍ' ELSE 'NO' END AS AceptaNulos, SCHEMA_NAME(t.schema_id) 
FROM sys.columns c 
JOIN sys.types ty 
ON c.user_type_id = ty.user_type_id 
JOIN sys.tables t 
ON c.object_id = t.object_id 
WHERE t.name = 'N19CUEENVAPREMIOS' and SCHEMA_NAME(t.schema_id) = 'APREMIOS'
ORDER BY c.column_id;

---

JOIN sys.types ty 
ON c.user_type_id = ty.user_type_id 
JOIN sys.tables t 
ON c.object_id = t.object_id 
WHERE t.name = 'N19CUEENVAPREMIOS' and SCHEMA_NAME(t.schema_id) = 'APREMIOS'
ORDER BY c.column_id;
