SELECT 
    [Extent1].[COMUNA] AS [COMUNA], 
    [Extent1].[CODSISTEMA] AS [CODSISTEMA], 
    [Extent1].[DESCRIPCION] AS [DESCRIPCION], 
    [Extent1].[FECHAPUESTAMARCHA] AS [FECHAPUESTAMARCHA], 
    [Extent1].[RESPONSABLE] AS [RESPONSABLE], 
    [Extent1].[CODAPLICACION] AS [CODAPLICACION], 
    [Extent1].[SISTEMA_CUM] AS [SISTEMA_CUM], 
    [Extent1].[SISTEMA_CDP] AS [SISTEMA_CDP], 
    [Extent1].[COD_OFICINA] AS [COD_OFICINA], 
    [Extent1].[HORA_ALTA] AS [HORA_ALTA], 
    [Extent1].[FECHA_ALTA] AS [FECHA_ALTA], 
    [Extent1].[USUARIO_ALTA] AS [USUARIO_ALTA], 
    [Extent1].[HORA_UM] AS [HORA_UM], 
    [Extent1].[FECHA_UM] AS [FECHA_UM], 
    [Extent1].[USUARIO_UM] AS [USUARIO_UM], 
    [Extent1].[DENOREDU] AS [DENOREDU], 
    [Extent1].[DENOM_BOLETAS] AS [DENOM_BOLETAS], 
    [Extent1].[BOL_EMIS_PREIMPR] AS [BOL_EMIS_PREIMPR], 
    [Extent1].[BOL_REEMIS_PREIMPR] AS [BOL_REEMIS_PREIMPR], 
    [Extent1].[BOL_MJEMEDIOSDEPGO] AS [BOL_MJEMEDIOSDEPGO], 
    [Extent1].[BOL_MJEMEDPGOREEMI] AS [BOL_MJEMEDPGOREEMI], 
    [Extent1].[IMPR_PUBLIC] AS [IMPR_PUBLIC], 
    [Extent1].[PATH_ARCH_PUBLIC] AS [PATH_ARCH_PUBLIC], 
    [Extent1].[VIG_DDE_MARC_CCT] AS [VIG_DDE_MARC_CCT], 
    [Extent1].[VIG_HTA_MARC_CCT] AS [VIG_HTA_MARC_CCT], 
    [Extent1].[VTO_ULTCTAAMARCCCT] AS [VTO_ULTCTAAMARCCCT], 
    [Extent1].[ORDEN_VIS_CTACTE] AS [ORDEN_VIS_CTACTE], 
    [Extent1].[PATH_QR] AS [PATH_QR]
    FROM (SELECT 
    [M00SISTE].[COMUNA] AS [COMUNA], 
    [M00SISTE].[CODSISTEMA] AS [CODSISTEMA], 
    [M00SISTE].[DESCRIPCION] AS [DESCRIPCION], 
    [M00SISTE].[FECHAPUESTAMARCHA] AS [FECHAPUESTAMARCHA], 
    [M00SISTE].[RESPONSABLE] AS [RESPONSABLE], 
    [M00SISTE].[CODAPLICACION] AS [CODAPLICACION], 
    [M00SISTE].[SISTEMA_CUM] AS [SISTEMA_CUM], 
    [M00SISTE].[SISTEMA_CDP] AS [SISTEMA_CDP], 
    [M00SISTE].[COD_OFICINA] AS [COD_OFICINA], 
    [M00SISTE].[HORA_ALTA] AS [HORA_ALTA], 
    [M00SISTE].[FECHA_ALTA] AS [FECHA_ALTA], 
    [M00SISTE].[USUARIO_ALTA] AS [USUARIO_ALTA], 
    [M00SISTE].[HORA_UM] AS [HORA_UM], 
    [M00SISTE].[FECHA_UM] AS [FECHA_UM], 
    [M00SISTE].[USUARIO_UM] AS [USUARIO_UM], 
    [M00SISTE].[DENOREDU] AS [DENOREDU], 
    [M00SISTE].[DENOM_BOLETAS] AS [DENOM_BOLETAS], 
    [M00SISTE].[BOL_EMIS_PREIMPR] AS [BOL_EMIS_PREIMPR], 
    [M00SISTE].[BOL_REEMIS_PREIMPR] AS [BOL_REEMIS_PREIMPR], 
    [M00SISTE].[BOL_MJEMEDIOSDEPGO] AS [BOL_MJEMEDIOSDEPGO], 
    [M00SISTE].[BOL_MJEMEDPGOREEMI] AS [BOL_MJEMEDPGOREEMI], 
    [M00SISTE].[IMPR_PUBLIC] AS [IMPR_PUBLIC], 
    [M00SISTE].[PATH_ARCH_PUBLIC] AS [PATH_ARCH_PUBLIC], 
    [M00SISTE].[VIG_DDE_MARC_CCT] AS [VIG_DDE_MARC_CCT], 
    [M00SISTE].[VIG_HTA_MARC_CCT] AS [VIG_HTA_MARC_CCT], 
    [M00SISTE].[VTO_ULTCTAAMARCCCT] AS [VTO_ULTCTAAMARCCCT], 
    [M00SISTE].[ORDEN_VIS_CTACTE] AS [ORDEN_VIS_CTACTE], 
    [M00SISTE].[PATH_QR] AS [PATH_QR]
    FROM [dbo].[M00SISTE] AS [M00SISTE]) AS [Extent1]
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA,NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 01/01/1900, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, CHR(0), 
FECHA_CANCEL, 0
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND
COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND
(TIPOJUICIO <> 'O' AND TIPOJUICIO <> 'C')
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA,NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 01/01/1900, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, CHR(0), 
FECHA_CANCEL, 0
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND
COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND
(TIPOJUICIO <> 'O' AND TIPOJUICIO <> 'C');

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 
AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND 
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 01/01/1900, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, CHR(0), 
FECHA_CANCEL, 0
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND
COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND
(TIPOJUICIO <> 'O' AND TIPOJUICIO <> 'C');

FECHA_CANCEL, 0

WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 
AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND 
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC

FECHA_CANCEL, 0

WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND

COD_CANCELAC = '' AND
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND
(TIPOJUICIO <> 'O' AND TIPOJUICIO <> 'C');

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900', NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, CHR(0),
FECHA_CANCEL, 0 
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '12/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 
AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND 
FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
ORDER BY CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 01/01/1900, NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, false, FECHA_CANCEL, 0
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/014/2025' AND '15/01/2026'' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND
(COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION. COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN 
(SELECT M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA, M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO, M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION, M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA, M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO 
FROM M10TABCLA WHERE COD_COMUNA = M10TABCLA.COD_COMUNA) AND
COD_JURISDICCION = M10TABCLA.COD_JUZGADO AND 
COD_INSTANCIA = M10TABCLA.DESCRIPCION AND 
AÑO_DEMANDA = M10TABCLA.ANODEMANDA AND
NRO_JUICIO = M10TABCLA.NROJUICIO AND
M10TABCLA.CODSISTEMA = 3)
 AND
TIPOJUICIO = ''
---

FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND

WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
(11=11) and
(COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN 
(SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
FROM M10TABCLA M
WHERE COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
COD_JURISDICCION = M.COD_JUZGADO AND 
COD_INSTANCIA = M.DESCRIPCION AND 
AÑO_DEMANDA = M.ANODEMANDA AND
NRO_JUICIO = M.NROJUICIO AND
M.CODSISTEMA = 3) AND 

COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND 

TIPOJUICIO = ''
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900', NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, 0, FECHA_CANCEL, 0
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND

(COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN 
(SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
FROM M10TABCLA M
WHERE COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
COD_JURISDICCION = M.COD_JUZGADO AND 
COD_INSTANCIA = M.DESCRIPCION AND 
AÑO_DEMANDA = M.ANODEMANDA AND
NRO_JUICIO = M.NROJUICIO AND
M.CODSISTEMA = 3) AND 

COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND 

TIPOJUICIO = ''
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                     AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, 
                   MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
                   AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = ?
                                     AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, CODSISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, '01/01/1900', NOMBRE, CUIJ_J, 0, FECHA_CANCEL, 0
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 99999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND

(COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN 
(SELECT M.COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JUZGADO, M.DESCRIPCION, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
FROM M10TABCLA M
WHERE COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND

COD_INSTANCIA = M.DESCRIPCION AND

M.CODSISTEMA = 3) AND 

COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND 

(COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN 
(SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, 
                   MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
                   AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = ?
                                     AND COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' 
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 AND 

(COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN 
(SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, MT.NROJUICIO 
FROM M10TABCLA MT 
WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND 
COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND 
COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND 
NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND 
MT.CODSISTEMA = 3 AND 

COD_CANCELAC = '' AND FECHA_CANCEL = '01/01/1900' AND 

TIPOJUICIO = ''
ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---

                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
                                    COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
                                    NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999.99 
                                     AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                    FROM M10ESTJU WHERE FECHATRAMITEJUIC BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '15/01/2026')
                                     AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA,

                   AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = 3)
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC

                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = 1 AND

                                    (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN

SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE COD_ESTADO IN ('2','4') AND  
                                            NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 0
---
SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (2,4) AND  
                                            NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 0
---
SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (1,3) AND  
                                            NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 2
---
SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (1,3) AND  
                                            NROJUICIO > 0 AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > 0 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 2
---
SELECT M.CODCOMUNA, M.JURISDICCION, M.INSTANCIA, M.ANODEMANDA, M.NROJUICIO 
                                            FROM M10ESTJU M
                                            WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (1,3) AND  
                                            NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                                            COD_ESTADO > ? 
                                            GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO 
                                            HAVING COUNT (*) > 2
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                    FROM M10ESTJU WHERE COD_ESTADO IN ('1','3') AND NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                    COD_ESTADO > ?  
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 2) AS T  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = '' AND T.CODCOMUNA = J.COD_COMUNA AND T.JURISDICCION = J.COD_JURISDICCION AND T.INSTANCIA = J.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
                    T.ANODEMANDA = J.AÑO_DEMANDA AND T.NROJUICIO = J.NRO_JUICIO
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                    FROM M10ESTJU WHERE COD_ESTADO IN ('1','3') AND NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                    COD_ESTADO > ?  
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 2) AS T  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = '' AND T.CODCOMUNA = J.COD_COMUNA AND T.JURISDICCION = J.COD_JURISDICCION AND T.INSTANCIA = J.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
                    T.ANODEMANDA = J.AÑO_DEMANDA AND T.NROJUICIO = J.NRO_JUICIO
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC
---
SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                    FROM M10ESTJU WHERE COD_ESTADO IN ('1','3') AND NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                    COD_ESTADO > ?  
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 2
---
SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
                    FROM M10ESTJU WHERE COD_ESTADO IN ('1','3') AND NROJUICIO > ? AND 
                    COD_ESTADO > ?  
                    GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ?

                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND

                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ?

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = '' AND

                                     RTRIM(CHAR(COD_JURISDICCION)) || '_' ||

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = '' AND

                                     RTRIM(CHAR(AÑO_DEMANDA)) || '_' ||

                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = '' AND 

                                     T.CODCOMUNA = J.COD_COMUNA AND 
                                     T.JURISDICCION = J.COD_JURISDICCION AND 
                                     T.INSTANCIA = J.COD_INSTANCIA AND 
                                     T.ANODEMANDA = J.AÑO_DEMANDA AND 
                                     T.NROJUICIO = J.NRO_JUICIO
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J , 
(SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO FROM (SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, 
INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO 
FROM M10ESTJU 
WHERE COD_ESTADO IN (1, 3) AND 
NROJUICIO > ? AND 
COD_ESTADO > ?  
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO) AS CE 
GROUP BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO HAVING COUNT(*) = 2) AS T  

                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '16/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = '' AND 

                                     T.CODCOMUNA = J.COD_COMUNA AND 
                                     T.JURISDICCION = J.COD_JURISDICCION AND 
                                     T.INSTANCIA = J.COD_INSTANCIA AND

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '18/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                     AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, 
                   MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
                   AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = ?)
                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC

         WHERE RELOJ_77 = 31 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 
         BETWEEN '12/01/2026' AND '19/01/2026' 
ORDER BY FECHA_PARTE_77 DESC;

         WHERE RELOJ_77 = 31 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 
         BETWEEN '12/01/2025' AND '19/01/2025'

         WHERE RELOJ_77 = 1 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77

FROM W12FECHA
WHERE FEC_LEVAN_FICH_77 = '01/01/1900' AND FECHA_1_PROC_77 = '01/01/1900'

FROM W12FECHA
         WHERE RELOJ_77 = 0 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 BETWEEN '01/01/2021' AND '02/01/2021'

FROM W12FECHA
         WHERE RELOJ_77 = 0 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 BETWEEN '01/01/2021' AND '02/01/2021'

UPDATE W12FECHA SET FECHA_1_PROC_77 = FECHA_PARTE_77, FECHA_ULT_PROC_77 = FECHA_PARTE_77
WHERE RELOJ_77 = 0 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 BETWEEN '01/01/2021' AND '02/01/2021' 

---
SELECT * 
FROM W12FECHA
         WHERE RELOJ_77 = 0 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 BETWEEN '01/01/2021' AND '02/01/2021' 


---

WHERE RELOJ_77 = 0 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 BETWEEN '01/01/2021' AND '02/01/2021'

WHERE RELOJ_77 = 0 AND 
         FECHA_PARTE_77 BETWEEN '01/01/2021' AND '02/01/2021'

SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA AS INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO, NRO_JUICIO AS JUICIO, CODSISTEMA AS SISTEMA, 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL AS MONTO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_ULT_MOV, NOMBRE AS DEMANDADO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, FECHA_CANCEL AS FECHA_CANCELACION, 0 AS MONTO_CANCELADO
                                    FROM JUICIOSPORSISTEMA J  
                                    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
                                    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '18/01/2026' AND 
                                    MONTO_INICIAL BETWEEN ? AND ? 
                                    
                                     AND (COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO) IN (SELECT MT.COD_COMUNA, MT.COD_JUZGADO, MT.DESCRIPCION, MT.ANODEMANDA, 
                   MT.NROJUICIO FROM M10TABCLA MT WHERE COD_COMUNA = MT.COD_COMUNA AND COD_JURISDICCION = MT.COD_JUZGADO AND COD_INSTANCIA = MT.DESCRIPCION AND 
                   AÑO_DEMANDA = MT.ANODEMANDA AND NRO_JUICIO = MT.NROJUICIO AND MT.CODSISTEMA = ?)
-- Parametro TIPO JUICIO                                    
                                     AND TIPOJUICIO = ''
                                     ORDER BY SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA ASC

SELECT COMUNA_J, 
	CASE WHEN CONVENIO_J = 0 THEN CUENTA_J ELSE 0 END, 
	CASE WHEN CONVENIO_J = 0 THEN SUBCTA_J ELSE 0 END,
	CASE WHEN CONVENIO_J = 0 THEN SISTEMA_J ELSE 4 END,
	CASE WHEN CONVENIO_J = 0 THEN SUBSIST_J ELSE 0 END,
	CONVENIO_J, NROINTER_J, JURISDIC_J, INSTANCIA_J, ANDEMAN_J, NROJUICIO_J, 0, MONTOAC_J, '', '', '', FGRABAC_J, USUARIO_J, '01/01/1900'
FROM M10JUINT 
WHERE COMUNA_J = ? AND 
FGRABAC_J BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
USUARIO_J = 'SSNUNEZ' AND 
FBAJA_J > '01/01/1900 ' AND 
NROJUICIO_J = 0

	CONVENIO_J AS CONVENIO, NROINTER_J AS NRO_JUICIO_INTERNO, JURISDIC_J AS JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA_J AS INSTANCIA, 
	ANDEMAN_J AS ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO_J AS NRO_JUICIO_DEF, 0 AS NRO_GESTION_COB, MONTOAC_J AS TOTAL_DEUDA_A_APR, '' AS TITULAR, 
	'' AS DOMICILIOCOBRO, '' AS DOMICILIOINMUEBLE, FGRABAC_J AS FECHA_ENVIO, USUARIO_J AS USUARIO_ENVIO, '01/01/1900' AS FECHA_UL_VENCI, CuotasEnvOrig, ImpActEnvOrig

WHERE COMUNA_J = ? AND

        CASE WHEN CONVENIO_J = 0 THEN CHAR(CUENTA_J) || ' ' || CHAR(SUBCTA_J) ELSE CHAR(CONVENIO_J) END AS CLAVE
    FROM M10JUINT 
    WHERE COMUNA_J = 1 AND 
    FGRABAC_J BETWEEN '23/01/2025' AND '23/01/2025' AND 
    FBAJA_J = '01/01/1900'
GROUP BY FECHA_ENVIO

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, FECHA_DEMANDA, CUIJ_J 
    FROM M10NAPLEG
    WHERE NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
    TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/11/2025' AND
    ORDER BY COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, FECHA_DEMANDA, CUIJ_J 
    FROM M10NAPLEG
    WHERE NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
    TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/11/2025'
    ORDER BY COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, FECHA_DEMANDA, CUIJ_J 
    FROM M10NAPLEG
    WHERE NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
    TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/11/2025'
    ORDER BY COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO;
    
SELECT COD_ESTADO, DESCRIPCION, FECHATRAMITEJUIC
        FROM (
            SELECT
                CODCOMUNA,
                JURISDICCION,
                INSTANCIA,
                ANODEMANDA,
                NROJUICIO,
                COD_ESTADO,
                DESCRIPCION,
                FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
                ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
                   PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
                   ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                ) AS RN
            FROM M10ESTJU
            WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
              AND NROJUICIO = 21242104983 AND ANODEMANDA = 2025 AND JURISDICCION = 1 AND INSTANCIA = 1
        ) X
        WHERE RN = 1
          AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
        ORDER BY
            CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO  
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, FECHA_DEMANDA, CUIJ_J 
    FROM M10NAPLEG
    WHERE NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
    TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/11/2025'
    ORDER BY COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO;
    
SELECT COD_ESTADO, DESCRIPCION, FECHATRAMITEJUIC
        FROM (
            SELECT
                CODCOMUNA,
                JURISDICCION,
                INSTANCIA,
                ANODEMANDA,
                NROJUICIO,
                COD_ESTADO,
                DESCRIPCION,
                FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
                ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
                   PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
                   ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                ) AS RN
            FROM M10ESTJU
            WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
              AND ANODEMANDA = 2025 AND JURISDICCION = 1 AND INSTANCIA = 1
        ) X
        WHERE RN = 1
          AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
        ORDER BY
            CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, FECHA_DEMANDA, CUIJ_J 
    FROM M10NAPLEG
    WHERE NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND
    TIPOJUICIO = '' AND
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/11/2025'
    ORDER BY COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO;
    
SELECT NROJUICIO, COD_ESTADO, DESCRIPCION, FECHATRAMITEJUIC
        FROM (
            SELECT
                CODCOMUNA,
                JURISDICCION,
                INSTANCIA,
                ANODEMANDA,
                NROJUICIO,
                COD_ESTADO,
                DESCRIPCION,
                FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
                ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
                   PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
                   ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                ) AS RN
            FROM M10ESTJU
            WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
              AND ANODEMANDA = 2025 AND JURISDICCION = 1 AND INSTANCIA = 1
        ) X
        WHERE RN = 1
          AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
        ORDER BY
            CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO  
---
SELECT NROJUICIO, ANODEMANDA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, COD_ESTADO, DESCRIPCION, FECHATRAMITEJUIC
        FROM (
            SELECT
                CODCOMUNA,
                JURISDICCION,
                INSTANCIA,
                ANODEMANDA,
                NROJUICIO,
                COD_ESTADO,
                DESCRIPCION,
                FECHATRAMITEJUIC,
                ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
                   PARTITION BY CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO
                   ORDER BY FECHATRAMITEJUIC DESC
                ) AS RN
            FROM M10ESTJU
            WHERE FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
        ) X
        WHERE RN = 1
          AND (DAYS(CURRENT DATE) - DAYS(FECHATRAMITEJUIC)) >= 10
        ORDER BY

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 
	COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA,CUIJ_J 
	FROM M10NAPLEG  
	WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/01/2026' and 
	COD_INSTANCIA between 1 and 9 and 
	FECHA_DEMANDA between '01/01/2025' AND '30/01/2026'
	AND NOT(TIPOJUICIO ='O')
ORDER BY M10NAPLEG.FECHA_CANCEL, M10NAPLEG.COD_COMUNA, M10NAPLEG.COD_JURISDICCION

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 
	COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J

SELECT COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, 
	COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J
	FROM M10NAPLEG
	WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/01/2026' AND 
	COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
	FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '30/01/2026'
ORDER BY FECHA_CANCEL, COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION
---
SELECT RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_INSTANCIA)) AS NRO_JUICIO_INSTANCIA, 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
    M.COD_COMUNA AS COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO_DEMANDA, 
    M.NRO_JUICIO AS NRO_JUICIO, T.CODSISTEMA AS CODSISTEMA, T.NROACTAS AS CLAVE_SISTEMA
    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10TABCLA T
    ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
    T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
    T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
    T.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
    T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO AND 
    T.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
    WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
    M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '31/01/2026' AND 
    M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
    M.TIPOJUICIO = ''
    
---
SELECT RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_INSTANCIA)) AS NRO_JUICIO_INSTANCIA, 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
    M.COD_COMUNA AS COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO_DEMANDA, 
    M.NRO_JUICIO AS NRO_JUICIO, T.CODSISTEMA AS CODSISTEMA, T.NROACTAS AS CLAVE_SISTEMA
    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10TABCLA T
    ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
    T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
    T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
    T.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
    T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO AND 
    T.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
    WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
    M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '31/01/2026' AND 
    M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
    M.TIPOJUICIO = ' '
    
---
SELECT RTRIM(CHAR(DECIMAL(M.NRO_JUICIO, 12,0))) || '/' || RTRIM(CHAR(M.COD_INSTANCIA)) AS NRO_JUICIO_INSTANCIA, 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA AS FECHA_DEMANDA, M.MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, M.CUIJ_J AS CUIJ, 
    M.COD_COMUNA AS COD_COMUNA, M.COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, M.COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, M.AÑO_DEMANDA AS AÑO_DEMANDA, 
    M.NRO_JUICIO AS NRO_JUICIO, T.CODSISTEMA AS CODSISTEMA, T.NROACTAS AS CLAVE_SISTEMA
    FROM M10NAPLEG M
    JOIN M10TABCLA T
    ON T.COD_COMUNA = M.COD_COMUNA AND
    T.DESCRIPCION = M.COD_INSTANCIA AND
    T.COD_JUZGADO =  M.COD_JURISDICCION AND
    T.ANODEMANDA = M.AÑO_DEMANDA AND
    T.NROJUICIO = M.NRO_JUICIO AND 
    T.FECHA_BAJA = '01/01/1900'
    WHERE M.COD_COMUNA = 1 AND 
    M.COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
    M.FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2025' AND '28/02/2026' AND 
    M.NRO_JUICIO BETWEEN 1 AND 999999999999 AND 
    M.TIPOJUICIO = ' '
    
---
SELECT  COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, 
NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J
FROM M10NAPLEG  
WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2024' AND '30/01/2026' 
AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2024' AND '30/01/2026' AND 
NOT(TIPOJUICIO = 'O')  
ORDER BY M10NAPLEG.FECHA_CANCEL, M10NAPLEG.COD_COMUNA, M10NAPLEG.COD_JURISDICCION
---
-- CONSULTA MAGIC
SELECT  COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, NOMBRE, FECHA_DEMANDA, MONTO_INICIAL, COD_CANCELAC, MONTO_ACT_DEUDA, FECHA_CANCEL, NRO_CONVENIO, 
NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J
FROM M10NAPLEG  
WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2024' AND '30/01/2026' 
AND COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2024' AND '30/01/2026' AND 
NOT(TIPOJUICIO = 'O')  
ORDER BY FECHA_CANCEL, COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION;

NRO_OFICGTOS, NRO_RECGTOS, NRO_OFICDEUDA, NRO_RECDEUDA, CUIJ_J

WHERE FECHA_CANCEL BETWEEN '01/01/2024' AND '30/01/2026' AND 
COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN 1 AND 9 AND 
FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/01/2024' AND '30/01/2026'

SELECT CODCOMUNA, JURISDICCION, INSTANCIA, ANODEMANDA, NROJUICIO, FECHATRAMITEJUIC, DESCRIPCION 
                                                FROM M10ESTJU 
                                                WHERE CODCOMUNA = ? AND
                                                JURISDICCION = ? AND
                                                INSTANCIA = ? AND
                                                ANODEMANDA = ? AND
                                                NROJUICIO = ?
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA,
    MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, TIPOJUICIO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND 
    COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/10/2025' AND '28/02/2026' AND 
    TIPOJUICIO = ''
    ORDER BY COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA,
    MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, TIPOJUICIO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND 
    COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/10/2025' AND '28/02/2026' AND 
    TIPOJUICIO = ''
    ORDER BY COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA
---
SELECT COD_COMUNA AS COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION AS INSTANCIA, COD_INSTANCIA AS JUZGADO, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO, COD_SISTEMA, FECHA_DEMANDA,
    MONTO_INICIAL AS TOTAL_DEMANDADO, TIPOJUICIO, CUIJ_J AS CUIJ
    FROM M10NAPLEG 
    WHERE COD_COMUNA = ? AND 
    COD_INSTANCIA BETWEEN ? AND ? AND 
    FECHA_DEMANDA BETWEEN '01/10/2025' AND '28/02/2026' AND 
    TIPOJUICIO = ''
    ORDER BY COD_SISTEMA, COD_COMUNA, COD_JURISDICCION, COD_INSTANCIA, AÑO_DEMANDA, NRO_JUICIO

SELECT * FROM N12HS_EXTRAS
WHERE LEGAJO_HX BETWEEN 1 AND 9999 AND
MESREALIZA_HX BETWEEN '01/01/2020' AND '30/09/2025' AND
COD_MOVIM_HX = 2 AND
SECRET_HX BETWEEN 1 AND 1 AND
SUBSECRET_HX BETWEEN 2 AND 2 AND
NIVEL01_HX BETWEEN 2 AND 2 AND
FECHBAJA_HX = '01/01/1900';

WHERE

SUBSECRETARIA_12 BETWEEN 2 AND 2 AND
NIVEL_1_12 BETWEEN 2 AND 2 AND
NIVEL_2_12 = 1

SELECT CODPRIN, SUBCOD, COMUNA, CODAPLICACION, CODSISTEMA, DENORE, DENOAM, FECDES, FECHAS, CAMPONUM1, CAMPONUM2, CAMPONUM3, CAMPONUM4, CODIGOS, CODALPHA2, CODALPHA3, CODALPHA4, CODALPHA5, CAAÑOS, CAMES, CADIA, FECALTA, USUALTA, FECMODI, USUMODI, FECBAJA, USUBAJA, ANULA 
FROM M00TABMA
WHERE CODPRIN = 500 AND SUBCOD = 1 AND FECBAJA = '01/01/1900'
---
SELECT CODPRIN, SUBCOD, COMUNA, CODAPLICACION, CODSISTEMA, DENORE, DENOAM, FECDES, FECHAS, CAMPONUM1, CAMPONUM2, CAMPONUM3, CAMPONUM4, CODIGOS, CODALPHA2, CODALPHA3, CODALPHA4, CODALPHA5, CAAÑOS, CAMES, CADIA, FECALTA, USUALTA, FECMODI, USUMODI, FECBAJA, USUBAJA, ANULA 
FROM M00TABMA
WHERE CODPRIN = 500  AND FECBAJA = '01/01/1900'
